msg:The room was quite clean. The service of the housekeeping lady was also good. I really like this.
The only thing I was very dissatisfied with was that the breakfast stall closed too early, at 9:30. We went there during the May Day holiday, and there were still many people in the restaurant at 9:30, and they started to close the food. It was not humane at all.
The location of this hotel tends to be a resort, and the environment is so good. Resort hotels usually close for breakfast at 10:30.
Because there are also lunch and lunch buffets! So they are in a hurry to close the food.
In fact, I also had the hotel's dinner buffet, and it was the same problem. The food was very slow. Many dishes were empty and they were called for a long time before they were served. The waiters who cooked in the restaurant had a stern face and were not willing to serve. They were not as enthusiastic as the housekeeping ladies.
The environment outside the hotel is very good.
In comparison, the food was not very comfortable.

msg:It was my first time to go to Binzhou. I valued the location of this hotel by the Zhonghai Lake. As a result, the environment was more beautiful than I could imagine. The willow trees were just green in early spring, the plank road curved into the lake, unknown water birds were playing in the lake, and a few seagulls were flying in the sky. It was natural, quiet, and healing.
The hotel service was also remarkable, and the waiters were polite and thoughtful. I was alone for dinner and wanted to order soup. The waiter said there was free porridge available. Great, the porridge was delicious, and I drank four bowls (small bowls) in a row. I asked the front desk to add two bottles of mineral water, and the waiter brought four bottles. Great.
I recommend everyone to stay in this hotel when you come to Binzhou. The environment is first-class and the service is great.
